2025-02-04 18:49:16 meilaleinalainen: # Staff-Guide
## Expectations of staff
**As a staff member you are expected to help create a safe and well-moderated environment. This includes enforcing the rules set within the FreeBuild, and the Discord.

### Supporter+ exclusive commands
`/dem <player>` - **Demotes affected player. Make sure to run **`/demlog`** afterwards**
`/clearninv <player>`  - **Clears all effects & inventory of a player.**
`/speedy` -** Applies **Speed** to you.**

### Staff+ exclusive commands
`/invis` - **Turns you invisible to look out for griefers.**
`/undercover` - **Disguises you as a **Build 2** rank to blend in with regular players.**
`/turnmeback` - **Grants your original rank back.

View all these cmds in game by doing /staffcmds
You are required to do /demlog after demoting someone

## Inactivity of Staff
### Due to security measures, we will lower your rank after a certain timeframe:
> 3 Weeks: You will be set to *Supporter* rank due to security measurements.
> 2 Months: Your rank will be set to *Build 3*

If you need to be inactive for a longer period of time, please let TiesKey know ü§†

2025-02-18 15:38:00 tieskey7: # Staff-Guide
## Expectations of staff
**As a staff member you are expected to help create a safe and well-moderated environment. This includes enforcing the rules set within the FreeBuild, and the Discord.

### Helper+ exclusive commands
`/dem <player>` - **Demotes affected player. Make sure to run **`/demlog`** afterwards**
`/clearninv <player>`  - **Clears all effects & inventory of a player.**
`/speedy` -** Applies **Speed** to you.**
`/nickick <player>` - Kicks a nicked player (Only use when you are certain a player is nicked)
### Staff+ exclusive commands
`/invis` - **Turns you invisible to look out for griefers.**
`/undercover` - **Disguises you as a **Build V** rank to blend in with regular players.**
`/promote <player>` - **Promotes a player** from demoted rank to **Build I.**
View all these cmds in game by doing /staffcmds
You are required to do /demlog after demoting someone

## Inactivity of Staff
### Due to security measures, we will lower your rank after a certain timeframe:
> 3 Weeks: You will be set to *Supporter* rank due to security measurements.
> 2 Months: Your rank will be set to *Build I*

If you need to be inactive for a longer period of time, please let me know ü§†

2025-02-28 16:13:58 TiesBot: # Tickets
### You can use this ticket program for support on your questions / appeals
Please only use this ticketing tool for the following things:

### Appeals:
 - You can create a ticket to appeal your in-game demotion / mute
 - There is a 14 day cooldown if your previous appeal has been rejected
 - Every appeal must include the reason you were demoted and your in-game user.

### Questions and general support:
 - If your question / issue doesnt get answered by <#1336130530156089398> or asking in <#1343609128538341479> and can't find an answer anywhere else, please create a ticket
### What not to create a ticket for:
 - Staff applications, please do that in <#1336134975426396223> 
 - Ban appeals
 - Non freebuild or Discord related questions

Please keep in mind that we may take up to 24 hours to respond to tickets.
